}</style><script>document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.clickable-card');
    
    cards.forEach(card => {
        const mainLink = card.querySelector('.loop-title a');
        const clickableElements = Array.from(card.querySelectorAll('a'));
        
        // Diğer linklere tıklanınca event'i durdur
        clickableElements.forEach(ele => 
            ele.addEventListener('click', e => e.stopPropagation())
        );
        
        // Card'a tıklanınca
        function handleClick(event) {
            const noTextSelected = !window.getSelection().toString();
            
            if (noTextSelected && mainLink) {
                mainLink.click();
            }
        }
        
        card.addEventListener('click', handleClick);
    });
});

			<script>
			(function($) {
				var uid = '2a17bdd';
				var $container = $('#wfs-container-' + uid);
				var $input = $('#wfs-input-' + uid);
				var $loader = $('#wfs-loader-' + uid);
				var $results = $('#wfs-results-' + uid);
				var $resultsWrapper = $('#wfs-results-wrapper-' + uid);
				var $noResults = $('#wfs-no-results-' + uid);
				var $description = $('#wfs-description-' + uid);
				var $quickLinks = $('#wfs-quick-links-' + uid);
				var $viewAll = $('#wfs-view-all-' + uid);

				var ajaxUrl = 'https://indirgo.club/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php';
				var timer;
				var minChars = 2;
				var showImage = 'yes' === 'yes';
				var showCategory = 'yes' === 'yes';
				var showPrice = '' === 'yes';
				var showViewAll = '' === 'yes';

				var currentRequest = null;

				// Search Logic
				$input.on('input', function() {
					var term = $(this).val().trim();
					clearTimeout(timer);

					if (currentRequest) {
						currentRequest.abort();
					}

					if (term.length < minChars) {
						hideResults();
						showBeforeSearch();
						$loader.removeClass('active complete');
						return;
					}

					$loader.addClass('active');
					hideBeforeSearch();

					timer = setTimeout(function() {
						currentRequest = $.ajax({
							url: ajaxUrl,
							data: {
								action: 'woo_fast_search',
								term: term
							},
							success: function(res) {
								// Complete the loader animation smoothly
								$loader.removeClass('active').addClass('complete');
								setTimeout(function() {
									$loader.removeClass('complete');
								}, 600);
								
								if (res.success && res.data.length > 0) {
									renderResults(res.data, term);
								} else {
									showNoResults();
								}
							},
							error: function(jqXHR) {
								if (jqXHR.statusText === 'abort') return;
								
								$loader.removeClass('active').addClass('complete');
								setTimeout(function() {
									$loader.removeClass('complete');
								}, 600);
								showNoResults();
							}
						});
					}, 150);
				});

				function renderResults(data, searchTerm) {
					var html = '';
					data.forEach(function(item) {
						var title = highlightText(item.t, searchTerm);
						html += '<a href="' + item.u + '" class="wfs-result-item">';
						if (showImage && item.i) {
							html += '<img src="' + item.i + '" alt="" class="wfs-result-image" loading="lazy">';
						}
						html += '<div class="wfs-result-content">';
						if (showCategory && item.c) {
							html += '<div class="wfs-result-cat">' + item.c + '</div>';
						}
						html += '<div class="wfs-result-title">' + title + '</div>';
						if (showPrice && item.type === 'product' && item.p) {
							html += '<div class="wfs-result-price">' + item.p + '</div>';
						}
						html += '</div>';
						html += '</a>';
					});
					$results.html(html);
					$resultsWrapper.show();
					$noResults.hide();

					// Update view all link
					if (showViewAll) {
						$viewAll.attr('href', '?s=' + encodeURIComponent(searchTerm) + '&post_type=product').show();
					}
				}

				function highlightText(text, term) {
					if (!term || term.length < 2) return text;

					var words = term.split(/\s+/).filter(function(w) { return w.length >= 2; });
					if (words.length === 0) return text;

					var patterns = words.map(function(w) {
						return createFlexibleRegex(w);
					});
					
					var regexStr = '(' + patterns.join('|') + ')';
					
					try {
						var regex = new RegExp(regexStr, 'gi');
						return text.replace(regex, '<span class="wfs-highlight">$1</span>');
					} catch(e) {
						return text;
					}
				}

				function createFlexibleRegex(term) {
					var substitutions = {
						'c': '[cçCÇ]', 'ç': '[cçCÇ]',
						'g': '[gğGĞ]', 'ğ': '[gğGĞ]',
						'i': '[iıİI]', 'ı': '[iıİI]',
						'o': '[oöOÖ]', 'ö': '[oöOÖ]',
						's': '[sşSŞ]', 'ş': '[sşSŞ]',
						'u': '[uüUÜ]', 'ü': '[uüUÜ]'
					};
					
					var pattern = '';
					for (var i = 0; i < term.length; i++) {
						var char = term[i].toLowerCase();
						if (substitutions[char]) {
							pattern += substitutions[char];
						} else {
							// Escape special regex chars
							if (['.','*','+','?','^','$','{','}','(',')','|','[',']','\\'].indexOf(term[i]) !== -1) {
								pattern += '\\' + term[i];
							} else {
								pattern += term[i];
							}
						}
					}
					return pattern;
				}

				function hideResults() {
					$resultsWrapper.hide();
					$noResults.hide();
					$viewAll.hide();
				}

				function showNoResults() {
					$resultsWrapper.hide();
					$noResults.show();
				}

				function showBeforeSearch() {
					$description.show();
					$quickLinks.show();
				}

				function hideBeforeSearch() {
					$description.hide();
					$quickLinks.hide();
				}

				// Focus input when container becomes visible (for off-canvas)
				var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
					mutations.forEach(function(mutation) {
						if (mutation.attributeName === 'class' || mutation.attributeName === 'style') {
							if ($container.is(':visible')) {
								setTimeout(function() {
									$input.focus();
								}, 300);
							}
						}
					});
				});

				// Observe parent for visibility changes
				var offCanvas = $container.closest('.elementor-widget-container').parent();
				if (offCanvas.length) {
					observer.observe(offCanvas[0], { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['class', 'style'] });
				}

				// Handle Quick Links Click
				$container.on('click', '.wfs-quick-link', function(e) {
					var $wrapper = $(this).closest('.wfs-quick-links');
					var action = $wrapper.data('action');
					
					if (action === 'populate') {
						e.preventDefault();
						var keyword = $(this).text().trim();
						$input.val(keyword).trigger('input').focus();
					}
				});

			})(jQuery);
			</script>
							</div>
				</div>
					</div>
				</div>
				</div>
						</div>
			</div>
		</nav>
						</div>

							<nav id="off-canvas-7f6e613" class="e-off-canvas" role="dialog" aria-hidden="true" aria-label="Menu" aria-modal="true" inert="" data-delay-child-handlers="true">

        (function() {
            function renderPendingPreview(wrapper, p, badgeText) {
                var list = wrapper.querySelector('.mcw-comment-list');
                if (!list) return;
                var noComments = list.querySelector('.mcw-no-comments');
                if (noComments) noComments.remove();
                var contentEscaped = (p.content || '').replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;').replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
                var initial = (p.author || '?').charAt(0).toUpperCase();
                var badgeEscaped = (badgeText || 'Onay bekliyor').replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
                var previewHtml = '<div class="mcw-comment mcw-comment-pending">' +
                    '<div class="mcw-comment-inner">' +
                    '<div class="mcw-avatar mcw-avatar-initial">' + initial + '</div>' +
                    '<div class="mcw-comment-body">' +
                    '<span class="mcw-pending-badge">' + badgeEscaped + '</span>' +
                    '<div class="mcw-comment-header">' +
                    '<span class="mcw-author-name">' + (p.author || '').replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;') + '</span>' +
                    '<span class="mcw-separator">·</span>' +
                    '<time class="mcw-comment-date">' + (p.date || '').replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;') + '</time>' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div class="mcw-comment-text">' + contentEscaped + '</div>' +
                    '</div></div></div>';
                list.insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', previewHtml);
            }

            // Reply button toggle
            document.querySelectorAll('.mcw-reply-btn').forEach(function(btn) {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    var commentId = btn.dataset.commentId;
                    var formWrapper = document.querySelector('.mcw-reply-form-wrapper[data-for-comment="' + commentId + '"]');
                    if (formWrapper) {
                        formWrapper.style.display = formWrapper.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
                    }
                });
            });

            // Cancel button
            document.querySelectorAll('.mcw-btn-cancel').forEach(function(btn) {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    var form = btn.closest('.mcw-comment-form');
                    var textarea = form.querySelector('.mcw-textarea');
                    if (textarea) textarea.value = '';

                    var replyWrapper = btn.closest('.mcw-reply-form-wrapper');
                    if (replyWrapper) {
                        replyWrapper.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                });
            });

            // Form submission via AJAX
            document.querySelectorAll('.mcw-comment-form').forEach(function(form) {
                form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();

                    var ajaxUrl = form.dataset.ajaxUrl;
                    if (!ajaxUrl) {
                        alert('AJAX URL bulunamadı.');
                        return;
                    }

                    var formData = new FormData(form);
                    var submitBtn = form.querySelector('.mcw-btn-submit');
                    var originalText = submitBtn.textContent;
                    submitBtn.textContent = 'Gönderiliyor...';
                    submitBtn.disabled = true;

                    // Convert FormData to URLSearchParams for proper encoding
                    var params = new URLSearchParams();
                    formData.forEach(function(value, key) {
                        params.append(key, value);
                    });

                    fetch(ajaxUrl, {
                            method: 'POST',
                            body: params,
                            credentials: 'same-origin',
                            headers: {
                                'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded'
                            }
                        })
                        .then(function(response) {
                            if (!response.ok) {
                                throw new Error('Network response was not ok');
                            }
                            return response.json();
                        })
                        .then(function(data) {
                            if (data.success) {
                                form.reset();
                                if (data.data.approved) {
                                    location.reload();
                                } else {
                                    var replyWrap = form.closest('.mcw-reply-form-wrapper');
                                    if (replyWrap) replyWrap.style.display = 'none';
                                    var wrapper = form.closest('.mcw-wrapper');
                                    var list = wrapper ? wrapper.querySelector('.mcw-comment-list') : null;
                                    var msg = (wrapper && wrapper.dataset.pendingMessage) ? wrapper.dataset.pendingMessage : 'Yorumunuz gönderildi. Yönetici onayından sonra yayınlanacaktır.';
                                    var badgeText = (wrapper && wrapper.dataset.pendingBadge) ? wrapper.dataset.pendingBadge : 'Onay bekliyor';
                                    if (data.data.preview && list) {
                                        renderPendingPreview(wrapper, data.data.preview, badgeText);
                                    }
                                    var notice = document.createElement('p');
                                    notice.className = 'mcw-success-notice';
                                    notice.textContent = msg;
                                    var formWrapper = wrapper ? wrapper.querySelector('.mcw-form-wrapper') : null;
                                    if (formWrapper && !formWrapper.querySelector('.mcw-success-notice')) {
                                        formWrapper.insertBefore(notice, formWrapper.firstChild);
                                        setTimeout(function() { notice.style.opacity = '0'; setTimeout(function() { notice.remove(); }, 300); }, 5000);
                                    }
                                }
                            } else {
                                alert(data.data && data.data.message ? data.data.message : 'Bir hata oluştu.');
                            }
                        })
                        .catch(function(error) {
                            console.error('MCW Error:', error);
                            alert('Bağlantı hatası: ' + error.message);
                        })
                        .finally(function() {
                            submitBtn.textContent = originalText;
                            submitBtn.disabled = false;
                        });
                });
            });
        })();
    </script>
    <script>
        (function() {
            document.querySelectorAll('.indirgo-read-more-btn').forEach(function(btn) {
                btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    var wrapper = btn.closest('.indirgo-post-content-wrapper');
                    var content = wrapper.querySelector('.indirgo-post-content');
                    var overlay = wrapper.querySelector('.indirgo-fade-overlay');
                    var isCollapsed = content.classList.contains('is-collapsed');

                    if (isCollapsed) {
                        content.classList.remove('is-collapsed');
                        content.classList.add('is-expanded');
                        if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'none';
                        btn.textContent = btn.dataset.less;
                    } else {
                        content.classList.add('is-collapsed');
                        content.classList.remove('is-expanded');
                        if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'block';
                        btn.textContent = btn.dataset.more;
                        // Scroll to top of content
                        wrapper.scrollIntoView({
                            behavior: 'smooth',
                            block: 'start'
                        });
                    }
                });
            });
        })();
    </script>

			stretchElement: null,
			getDefaultSettings: function() { return { selectors: { menu: '.elementor-nav-menu', anchorLink: '.elementor-nav-menu--main .elementor-item-anchor', dropdownMenu: '.elementor-nav-menu__container.elementor-nav-menu--dropdown', menuToggle: '.elementor-menu-toggle', overlay: '.elementor-nav-menu--overlay' } }; },
			getDefaultElements: function() { var selectors = this.getSettings('selectors'), elements = {}; elements.$menu = this.$element.find(selectors.menu); elements.$anchorLink = this.$element.find(selectors.anchorLink); elements.$dropdownMenu = this.$element.find(selectors.dropdownMenu); elements.$dropdownMenuFinalItems = elements.$dropdownMenu.find('.menu-item:not(.menu-item-has-children) > a'); elements.$menuToggle = this.$element.find(selectors.menuToggle); elements.$links = elements.$dropdownMenu.find('a.elementor-item'); elements.$overlay = this.$element.find(selectors.overlay); return elements; },
			bindEvents: function() { if (!this.elements.$menu.length) { return; } this.elements.$menuToggle.on('click', this.toggleMenu.bind(this)); if (this.getElementSettings('full_width')) { this.elements.$dropdownMenuFinalItems.on('click', this.toggleMenu.bind(this, false)); } if (this.elements.$overlay.length) { this.elements.$overlay.on('click', this.toggleMenu.bind(this, false)); } elementorFrontend.addListenerOnce(this.$element.data('model-cid'), 'resize', this.stretchMenu); },

    <script id="nextmerce-mobile-infinite-scroll">
    (function() {
        var mobileQuery = window.matchMedia('(max-width: 767px)');
        var observers = {};

        function initWidget(widget) {
            var trigger = widget.querySelector('.nextmerce-mobile-infinite-scroll-trigger[data-enabled="1"]');
            if (!trigger) return;
            var elementId = trigger.getAttribute('data-element-id');
            if (!elementId) return;
            var container = widget.querySelector('.elementor-loop-container');
            var anchor = widget.querySelector('.e-load-more-anchor');
            if (!container || !anchor) return;
            var nextPageUrl = anchor.getAttribute('data-next-page');
            if (!nextPageUrl) return;
            var dataPage = parseInt(anchor.getAttribute('data-page'), 10) || 1;
            var dataMaxPage = parseInt(anchor.getAttribute('data-max-page'), 10) || 1;
            if (dataPage >= dataMaxPage) return;

            var isLoading = false;
            var key = 'nextmerce-mobile-inf-' + elementId;
            if (observers[key]) {
                observers[key].disconnect();
                delete observers[key];
            }

            observers[key] = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
                if (!mobileQuery.matches || isLoading) return;
                var entry = entries[0];
                if (!entry || !entry.isIntersecting) return;
                nextPageUrl = anchor.getAttribute('data-next-page');
                if (!nextPageUrl) return;
                dataPage = parseInt(anchor.getAttribute('data-page'), 10) || 1;
                dataMaxPage = parseInt(anchor.getAttribute('data-max-page'), 10) || 1;
                if (dataPage >= dataMaxPage) return;

                isLoading = true;
                fetch(nextPageUrl).then(function(r) { return r.text(); }).then(function(html) {
                    var parser = new DOMParser();
                    var doc = parser.parseFromString(html, 'text/html');
                    var selector = '[data-id="' + elementId + '"] .elementor-loop-container > .e-loop-item';
                    var newItems = doc.querySelectorAll(selector);
                    var responseAnchor = doc.querySelector('[data-id="' + elementId + '"] .e-load-more-anchor');
                    newItems.forEach(function(el) { container.appendChild(el); });
                    if (responseAnchor) {
                        anchor.setAttribute('data-page', responseAnchor.getAttribute('data-page') || (dataPage + 1));
                        anchor.setAttribute('data-next-page', responseAnchor.getAttribute('data-next-page') || '');
                        anchor.setAttribute('data-max-page', responseAnchor.getAttribute('data-max-page') || dataMaxPage);
                    }
                    if (typeof elementorFrontend !== 'undefined' && elementorFrontend.elementsHandler) {
                        elementorFrontend.elementsHandler.runReadyTrigger(widget);
                    }
                    if (typeof document.dispatchEvent === 'function') {
                        document.dispatchEvent(new Event('elementor/lazyload/observe'));
                    }
                    isLoading = false;
                }).catch(function() { isLoading = false; });
            }, { rootMargin: '200px', threshold: 0 });

            observers[key].observe(anchor);
        }

        function run() {
            if (!mobileQuery.matches) return;
            var widgets = document.querySelectorAll('.elementor-widget-loop-grid');
            widgets.forEach(initWidget);
        }

        function cleanup() {
            Object.keys(observers).forEach(function(k) {
                observers[k].disconnect();
            });
            observers = {};
        }

        if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', run);
        } else {
            run();
        }
        mobileQuery.addEventListener('change', function() {
            if (!mobileQuery.matches) cleanup();
            else run();
        });
        if (typeof jQuery !== 'undefined') {
            jQuery(document).on('elementor-pro/loop-builder/after-insert-posts', run);
        }
    })();
    </script>

</html>
